[<transition> -> . goto L ; , ; | V | while | for | if | input | print | L | goto | select | raise | rem | od]
[<select> -> . select <E> in <case> ni ; , ; | V | while | for | if | input | print | L | goto | select | raise | rem | od]
[<exception> -> . raise ; , ; | V | while | for | if | input | print | L | goto | select | raise | rem | od]
